 Senior journalist Madhusudan Anand said that in the early history of Hindi literature and journalism, there was no separation between journalism and literature
 achche lekhak hi patrkaar the yaa kahen ki achche patrkaar hi lekhak the

 He argued that once upon a time literature used to follow the society but now it is following it
 yah paristhitiyaan badalani hogi tabhi sahitya mashaal kaa kaam kar paaegaa or tabhi use anya madhyamon main apekshit sthaan mil paaegaa
 Critic Anant Vijay questioned the literature of today, apart from his predecessor speakers, and asked whether the stories and compositions being written today really come under the purview of literature? He said that when poor literature is written, who will print it? He also said that literature can now be written not only for printing but also through cinema and television
 unka suzav tha ki hamen yah vilaap band karke ki sahitya chapa nahin ja rahaa ke sthaan par acha lekhan kar use prakaashan ke liye vivash karnaa hoga

 vah yah bhi jaan rahaa he ki sahitya main bhi brading banane kaa madda he
 That is why there has been a sudden flood of literature festivals and literature has become mainstream in every publication
 yah pathak kii takat he
 He said that journalism may be with the market, but literature will always oppose the market
